# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="4a9ec-102">Tipos obsoletos en .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4a9ec-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>
<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="4a9ec-103">En las tablas de este artículo se muestran los tipos que están obsoletos en [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] y [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)] organizados por ensamblados.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4a9ec-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the [!INCLUDE[net_v45](../../../includes/net-v45-md.md)] and the [!INCLUDE[net_v46](../../../includes/net-v46-md.md)], organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4a9ec-104">Utilice los vínculos siguientes para ver una lista de tipos obsoletos y las alternativas recomendadas en cada ensamblado.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4a9ec-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4a9ec-105">Dado que estos tipos están en desuso, todos sus miembros también lo están.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4a9ec-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="4a9ec-106">Para obtener una lista de miembros obsoletos adicionales de la biblioteca de clases de .NET Framework, vea [Miembros obsoletos](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="4a9ec-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>
